is_mail($Tb){$va='[-a-z0-9!#$%&\'*+/=?^_`{|}~]';$Hb='[a-z0-9]([-a-z0-9]{0,61}[a-z0-9])';$Ne="$va+(\\.$va+)*@($Hb?\\.)+$Hb";return
